       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         “Your message said it was an emergency?” Chakotay questions, walking into Kathryn’s and finding her covered in flour.
        </p>
        <p>
         “Oh thank goodness you’re here!” she exclaims, emerging from the kitchen to embrace him, “I have this VIP I’m supposed to charm coming over and the replicator is down.”
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <!--summary-->
       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         She snaps up reflexively, eyes wide. “You think this is from
         <i>
          Charles
         </i>
         ?” The question leaves her lips before she’s able to think about it. She almost winces at how her voice squeaks, a step higher than usual.
        </p>
        <p>
         Jake scoffs. “This probably cost at least a hundred bucks, Amy. Who else would go Full Boyle on something as dumb as Secret Santa? Nobody takes precinct-wide gift exchanges this seriously. Like, I legit just went and got HR Jim candy from the vending machine.”
        </p>
        <p>
         A Christmas-themed Get Together fic separate from the canon timeline, feat. Pining!Amy and the art of thoughtful gift giving.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

She almost winces at how her voice squeaks, a step higher than usual.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;Jake scoffs. “This probably cost at least a hundred bucks, Amy. Who else would go Full Boyle on something as dumb as Secret Santa? Nobody takes precinct-wide gift exchanges this seriously. Like, I legit just went and got HR Jim candy from the vending machine.”&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;A Christmas-themed Get Together fic separate from the canon timeline, feat. Pining!Amy and the art of thoughtful gift giving.&lt;/p&gt;</textarea>

       <!--summary-->
       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         Soulmate AU where Jake and Amy communicate through writing letters to each other as they grow up.
        </p>
        <p>
         "Her soulmate is someone with incredibly messy writing, it’s so messy it almost escapes the lines and is difficult to read. Amy seriously doubts the ability of the soulmate council - or whatever group of people it is who somehow magically assign people to their soulmates - to accurately match people if they’ve matched her with someone who is already the polar opposite of her in hand-writing."
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <!--summary-->
       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         For someone whose job requires an unusually large amount of personal risk on a near daily basis, Amy Santiago has not dedicated much time considering how she might one day die. The vague assumption that it will probably happen on the job - via stray bullets or careening cars or massive explosions - has been enough to satisfy any musing.
        </p>
        <p>
         She never imagined doctor's visits or specialist consultations or diagnoses. She never imagined hospital gowns and thinning hair and chemotherapy.
        </p>
        <p>
         And she never, ever imagined
         <i>
          cancer.
         </i>
        </p>
       </blockquote>
       <h6 class="landmark heading">

          we'll face the worst
         </a>
        </li>
       </ul>

       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         Amy Santiago loves her new apartment. One bedroom, one bathroom, good neighborhood and decent rent. One thing she does not love? Her neighbors. More precisely, whoever lives in the apartment that shares a paper thin wall with hers.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         “This yazkan box is used in a Wellia celebration of thanks and prosperity. It simply scans the person holding it and shows you something you truly want to see!”
        </p>
        <p>
         “Ah yes!” he exclaims. “Whenever I open it, I see this Talaxian fire slug.”
        </p>
        <p>
         “You see a slug?” Tom snorts.
        </p>
       </blockquote>

       <h6 class="landmark heading">
        Summary
       </h6>
       <blockquote class="userstuff summary">
        <p>
         A few months after their return to the Alpha Quadrant, the Voyager crew come together to assist one of their own. Along the way they face a new threat from an old enemy...make a new friend...and say goodbye to an old one. Adventure, humor, romance and fun. J/C, P/T, K/OC. Enjoy.
        </p>
       </blockquote>
